# Prompts for Claude — Complete Library

This is a combined library of 5 guides — Personal Growth, Coach, Marketer, Ultimate, and Business Owner — where each `###` entry uses a Fill-in-the-blank / Question-based / Examples format so you can adapt every prompt to your own situation.

- Personal Growth Prompts for Claude
- The Coach's Prompts for Claude
- The Marketer's Prompts for Claude
- The Ultimate Prompts for Claude
- The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude (Parts 1–11)

---

<!-- ==================== NEXT GUIDE / PART ==================== -->

# 🌱 The Personal Growth Prompts for Claude

> **How to use this guide:** Copy any prompt below, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders with your own details, and paste it into Claude (free or paid).
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** give you structured, ready-to-use output.
> - **Question-based prompts** are great for exploring a topic or going deeper.

---

## 🧠 Personal Development

### 💰 Analyze finances

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Could you generate a financial forecast for [work area/individual] over the next [time frame], utilizing historical data [data]? Please ensure the forecast includes predictions for revenue, expenses, and profits.
- What are the foreseeable financial risks for [work area/individual] within the upcoming [time frame], and what measures can be taken to mitigate them?
- Please analyze the financial implications of [business decision] on [work area/individual] and offer suggestions for maximizing financial results.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the key financial ratios that can help assess a company's profitability and financial health?"
- "How can the cash flow statement provide insights into a company's liquidity and ability to meet its financial obligations?"
- "What factors should be considered when evaluating the risk and return of an investment opportunity?"
- "In what ways can financial analysis help identify potential areas for cost reduction and efficiency improvement within a business?"
- "Why is it important to analyze the working capital of a company and how does it impact its overall financial performance?"
- "What are the major components of a company's capital structure and how does it affect its financial stability?"
- "How can financial statement analysis aid in assessing the creditworthiness of a potential borrower?"
- "What are the implications of different valuation methods, such as discounted cash flow and comparable company analysis, on investment decisions?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Please analyze the financial implications of hiring two new contractors on my freelance design business and offer suggestions for maximizing financial results."

---

### 😎 Overcome challenges

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I'm currently facing [challenge] in my [personal/professional] life. Break this down into smaller, manageable steps and suggest a realistic action plan for the next [time frame].
- Act as a resilience coach. I'm struggling with [specific obstacle]. Ask me [number] clarifying questions, then help me reframe the situation and identify what's within my control.
- I keep getting stuck when [describe the recurring problem]. Help me diagnose the root cause and recommend [number] strategies to move past it.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are some proven frameworks for working through a difficult challenge step by step?"
- "How can I tell the difference between an obstacle I should push through and one I should walk away from?"
- "What mindset shifts help people stay motivated when progress feels slow?"
- "How can I build resilience so future setbacks affect me less?"
- "What questions should I ask myself when I feel overwhelmed by a problem?"
- "How do successful people typically respond to failure or rejection?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I'm currently facing burnout in my professional life. Break this down into smaller, manageable steps and suggest a realistic action plan for the next 30 days."

---

### 💻 Analyze personal values

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me clarify my core personal values. Here is some context about me: [describe your priorities, what energizes you, what frustrates you]. Suggest [number] values that seem central and explain why.
- I have to make a decision between [option A] and [option B]. Help me evaluate each option against the values I care about most: [list values].
- Based on these recent choices I've made — [describe choices] — what values do they reveal about me, and where might there be a conflict?

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What is a simple exercise for identifying my core personal values?"
- "How do personal values influence the decisions we make day to day?"
- "What's the difference between values I actually live by and values I only aspire to?"
- "How can I use my values to set better boundaries?"
- "How do I resolve a conflict between two values I both care about?"
- "How often should I revisit and re-evaluate my personal values?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I have to make a decision between taking a higher-paying job and staying in a role with more flexibility. Help me evaluate each option against the values I care about most: family time, growth, and financial security."

---

### 🌟 Recommend personal development

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I want to grow in the area of [skill/trait, e.g. confidence, communication, discipline]. Recommend a [time frame] personal development plan with concrete weekly actions.
- Based on my current situation — [describe where you are] — and my goal of [goal], suggest the [number] most impactful areas I should focus on developing first.
- Recommend a mix of books, habits, and practices that would help someone working on [area of growth].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the highest-leverage areas most people should invest in for personal growth?"
- "How do I choose what to work on when I want to improve in many areas at once?"
- "What does a realistic personal development routine look like for a busy person?"
- "How can I measure progress on something as fuzzy as personal growth?"
- "What are common mistakes people make when trying to better themselves?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I want to grow in the area of public speaking. Recommend a 90-day personal development plan with concrete weekly actions."

---

### 🎥 Feedback on projects

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Here is a project I'm working on: [paste or describe the project]. Give me honest, constructive feedback on its strengths, weaknesses, and [number] specific improvements.
- Review this [type of work, e.g. presentation, design, plan] as if you were [target audience/expert]. What would impress them and what would they push back on?
- I want to improve [project]. Act as a critical but supportive reviewer and prioritize your feedback from most to least important.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What's the best way to ask for feedback that actually helps me improve?"
- "How do I separate useful criticism from noise?"
- "What questions should I ask a reviewer to get more specific feedback?"
- "How can I give myself an objective critique of my own work?"
- "How do I act on feedback without losing my original vision?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Review this pitch deck as if you were a skeptical investor. What would impress them and what would they push back on?"

---

### ↩️ Provide feedback

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me give constructive feedback to [person/role] about [situation]. I want to be honest but kind. Draft what I could say.
- I need to deliver some difficult feedback about [issue]. Suggest a structure (e.g. situation–behavior–impact) and example wording.
- Rewrite this blunt feedback to be more constructive and motivating: [paste feedback].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What is a proven framework for giving feedback that lands well?"
- "How do I give critical feedback without making the other person defensive?"
- "How do I balance positive and negative feedback?"
- "What's the best way to give feedback to someone more senior than me?"
- "How can I make my feedback specific and actionable?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Help me give constructive feedback to a teammate who consistently misses deadlines. I want to be honest but kind. Draft what I could say."

---

### 🛠 Suggest creative outlets

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I'm looking for a creative outlet that fits [time available], [budget], and my interest in [topics/themes]. Suggest [number] options and why they might suit me.
- I feel creatively blocked in [area]. Suggest exercises or new outlets to reignite my creativity.
- Recommend low-pressure creative hobbies for someone who [describe personality/constraints].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are some creative outlets that are easy to start with little time or money?"
- "How does having a creative hobby benefit mental health and focus?"
- "How do I find a creative outlet that I'll actually stick with?"
- "What can I do when I feel creatively stuck or uninspired?"
- "How can I make time for creativity in a busy schedule?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I'm looking for a creative outlet that fits 30 minutes a day, a small budget, and my interest in storytelling. Suggest 5 options and why they might suit me."

### 🔝 Suggest development courses

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I want to learn [skill/topic] to [goal]. Suggest [number] types of courses or learning paths, from beginner to advanced, and what to look for in a good one.
- Based on my background in [field] and my goal of [goal], what courses or certifications would be most worth my time?
- Compare self-paced vs. structured courses for learning [skill], and recommend which suits someone who [describe learning style].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I choose a course that's actually worth the time and money?"
- "What's the best way to learn a new skill — courses, projects, or mentorship?"
- "How can I tell if a certification is respected in [industry]?"
- "How do I stay motivated to finish an online course?"
- "What free or affordable resources rival paid courses for [skill]?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I want to learn data analysis to move into a product role. Suggest 5 types of courses or learning paths, from beginner to advanced, and what to look for in a good one."

### 🧔 Help set personal goals

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me turn this vague intention — "[intention]" — into a clear, measurable goal with milestones over the next [time frame].
- I want to achieve [goal] by [deadline]. Break it into quarterly and weekly targets and identify the first three actions I should take.
- Review my goals: [list goals]. Are they realistic and well-balanced? Suggest how to refine them.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What makes a personal goal effective and achievable?"
- "How many goals should I focus on at once?"
- "What's the difference between outcome goals and process goals?"
- "How do I set goals that stay motivating over the long term?"
- "How should I handle a goal I'm falling behind on?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I want to run a half marathon by next spring. Break it into quarterly and weekly targets and identify the first three actions I should take."

### 🌻 Suggest growth resources

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Recommend the best books, podcasts, and tools for someone working on [area of growth].
- I have [time available] per week to invest in self-improvement around [topic]. Suggest a resource plan that fits.
- Curate a "starter pack" of resources for a beginner who wants to understand [topic].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the most recommended books for personal growth?"
- "How do I avoid 'consuming' self-help content without ever applying it?"
- "What's a good system for taking notes and acting on what I learn?"
- "How do I find credible resources versus hype?"
- "How can I build a sustainable learning habit?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Recommend the best books, podcasts, and tools for someone working on emotional intelligence."

### 💪 Analyze strengths

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Based on this about me — [describe experiences, what comes easily, what others praise] — help me identify my top [number] strengths and how to use them more.
- I want to build my career around my strengths. Here's what I'm good at: [list]. Suggest roles or directions that would leverage them.
- Help me spot strengths I might be undervaluing, given this background: [describe].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How can I identify my natural strengths?"
- "Is it better to develop my strengths or fix my weaknesses?"
- "How do I describe my strengths confidently without sounding arrogant?"
- "How can I apply my strengths to areas where I struggle?"
- "How do strengths show up differently at work versus in personal life?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Based on the fact that people always ask me to mediate disagreements and I love organizing events, help me identify my top 5 strengths and how to use them more."

---

### 👮 Provide career advice

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I'm a [current role] considering a move into [target role/field]. What steps, skills, and experiences should I build over the next [time frame]?
- Here's my situation: [describe role, goals, frustrations]. Act as a career coach and give me honest advice on my best next move.
- Help me prepare for [career decision, e.g. asking for a raise, switching industries]. What should I consider and how should I approach it?

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I know when it's time to change jobs or careers?"
- "What's the best way to make a career pivot without starting from scratch?"
- "How can I make myself more valuable in my current role?"
- "What questions should I ask myself before accepting a new job?"
- "How do I negotiate a raise or promotion effectively?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I'm a marketing coordinator considering a move into product management. What steps, skills, and experiences should I build over the next 12 months?"

## ⏳ Time-Management

### 📧 Send pre-written emails

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Write a reusable email template for [recurring situation, e.g. declining a meeting, following up]. Keep it [tone] and easy to personalize.
- Create [number] pre-written email templates I can keep on hand for [context, e.g. client onboarding, scheduling].
- Turn this message I send often — [paste] — into a clean, reusable template with placeholders.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "Which routine emails are worth turning into templates?"
- "How do I keep template emails from sounding robotic?"
- "What's a good structure for a quick, professional email?"
- "How can I organize and quickly access my email templates?"
- "How do I personalize a template fast without losing the time savings?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Write a reusable email template for following up after a sales call. Keep it warm but concise and easy to personalize."

---

### 📥 Manage email inbox

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I get around [number] emails a day and feel overwhelmed. Suggest a system to reach and maintain inbox zero.
- Help me design email folders/labels and rules for someone who handles [types of email].
- Give me a [time frame] plan to clear a backlog of [number] unread emails without missing anything important.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the most effective methods for managing a busy inbox?"
- "How do I decide what to reply to, archive, delegate, or delete?"
- "How can I stop email from constantly interrupting my focus?"
- "What's a realistic way to maintain inbox zero long term?"
- "How do I write replies faster without being careless?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I get around 80 emails a day and feel overwhelmed. Suggest a system to reach and maintain inbox zero."

---

### 💿 Optimize daily routines

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Here's my current daily routine: [describe]. Suggest changes to make it more productive and less draining.
- Design an ideal daily routine for a [role/lifestyle] who wants to prioritize [priorities].
- I have these fixed commitments — [list] — and want to fit in [goals]. Help me build a realistic daily structure.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the habits of a highly productive daily routine?"
- "How do I build a routine that survives busy or chaotic days?"
- "Should I be a morning person or design around my natural energy?"
- "How do I balance structure with flexibility in my day?"
- "What's the best way to start and end my workday?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Design an ideal daily routine for a remote software developer who wants to prioritize deep work and exercise."

---

### 🕰 Research time management

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Explain the [time-management method, e.g. Pomodoro, time-blocking, Eisenhower matrix] and how I'd apply it to [my situation].
- Compare [number] popular time-management techniques and recommend which fits someone who [describe].
- Summarize the key ideas from research on productivity and focus, with practical takeaways for [my role].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the most effective evidence-based time-management techniques?"
- "Why do most time-management systems fail, and how do I avoid that?"
- "How does multitasking affect productivity?"
- "What does research say about focus and attention?"
- "How do I choose a time-management method that fits my personality?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Explain the Eisenhower matrix and how I'd apply it to managing competing client requests."

---

### 🧠 Brainstorm time solutions

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I keep running out of time for [activity]. Brainstorm [number] practical ways to free up time for it.
- Here's where my time goes: [describe]. Identify the biggest time sinks and suggest solutions.
- Help me find creative ways to combine, delegate, or eliminate these tasks: [list].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are common hidden time-wasters people overlook?"
- "How can I free up an extra hour in my day?"
- "What tasks are usually worth delegating or automating?"
- "How do I protect time for what matters most?"
- "How can I say no to low-value commitments?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I keep running out of time for exercise. Brainstorm 10 practical ways to free up time for it."

### 🥃 Provide motivational quotes

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Give me [number] motivational quotes about [theme, e.g. perseverance, focus, starting].
- I'm feeling [emotion/situation]. Share a few quotes and a short reflection to help me reframe it.
- Create a set of original motivational one-liners I could use as daily reminders about [topic].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are some powerful quotes about discipline and consistency?"
- "How can I use motivational quotes without relying on them as a crutch?"
- "What quotes capture the idea of progress over perfection?"
- "Which quotes help when facing fear or self-doubt?"
- "How do I turn a quote I love into an actual change in behavior?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I'm feeling discouraged after a setback. Share a few quotes and a short reflection to help me reframe it."

### 🤖 Automate repetitive tasks

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- These tasks eat up my week: [list]. Suggest ways to automate or streamline each one.
- I use [tools/apps]. Recommend automations or workflows to reduce manual work in [area].
- Help me design a simple checklist or template to speed up [recurring task].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I decide which tasks are worth automating?"
- "What everyday tasks can be automated with common apps?"
- "How do I start automating if I'm not technical?"
- "What's the difference between automating and simply eliminating a task?"
- "How do I avoid over-engineering my automations?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "These tasks eat up my week: scheduling social posts, sending invoices, and sorting receipts. Suggest ways to automate or streamline each one."

### ⏰ Generate time-saving hacks

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Give me [number] time-saving hacks for [activity/area, e.g. cooking, admin, commuting].
- I want to save time on [task]. Suggest shortcuts, tools, and habits to make it faster.
- What are some underrated time-saving tricks for a [role/lifestyle]?

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are simple time-saving habits with the biggest payoff?"
- "How can batching similar tasks save me time?"
- "What's the 80/20 rule and how do I apply it to my day?"
- "How do I save time without lowering quality?"
- "What small daily habits add up to big time savings?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Give me 10 time-saving hacks for handling household admin and errands."

### 🪡 Set up productivity system

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me design a personal productivity system using [tools I have]. I want to capture tasks, prioritize, and review weekly.
- I've tried [systems] and they didn't stick. Suggest a simpler system suited to someone who [describe].
- Walk me through setting up a [method, e.g. GTD, PARA] system step by step for [my context].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What makes a productivity system actually stick?"
- "How simple should my productivity system be?"
- "What's the difference between popular systems like GTD and time-blocking?"
- "How often should I review and adjust my system?"
- "How do I keep my system from becoming busywork?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Help me design a personal productivity system using Notion and my phone calendar. I want to capture tasks, prioritize, and review weekly."

### 🔭 Analyze time usage

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Here's how I spent my time this week: [describe/paste log]. Analyze where my time went and where I could improve.
- Help me create a simple way to track my time for [time frame] and what to look for in the results.
- I feel busy but unproductive. Ask me questions to help diagnose where my time is actually going.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What's the best way to track how I spend my time?"
- "How do I interpret a time audit to find improvements?"
- "Why do I feel busy but get little done?"
- "How much of my time should go to deep work versus admin?"
- "How often should I audit my time usage?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Here's how I spent my time this week: ~15 hours in meetings, 10 hours on email, 8 hours on actual project work. Analyze where my time went and where I could improve."

### 📕 Organize daily tasks and to-do lists

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Here's my brain-dump of tasks: [list]. Organize them by priority and suggest what to tackle today.
- Help me build a daily to-do list format that keeps me focused and not overwhelmed.
- Turn this messy list — [paste] — into a structured plan with categories and deadlines.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What's the best way to structure a daily to-do list?"
- "How many tasks should I realistically put on a daily list?"
- "How do I prioritize when everything feels urgent?"
- "How do I handle tasks that roll over day after day?"
- "Should I plan my day the night before or in the morning?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Here's my brain-dump of tasks: finish report, call dentist, plan team meeting, buy groceries, review budget. Organize them by priority and suggest what to tackle today."

### 🕧 Create a time-blocking system

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me build a time-blocking schedule for a typical week given these commitments and goals: [list].
- I want to try time-blocking for [area]. Walk me through how to set it up and avoid common pitfalls.
- Turn my to-do list — [list] — into a time-blocked day with realistic durations and buffers.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How does time-blocking work and who is it best for?"
- "How do I handle interruptions when time-blocking?"
- "How much buffer time should I leave between blocks?"
- "How do I time-block when my schedule is unpredictable?"
- "What's the difference between time-blocking and a regular to-do list?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Turn my to-do list — write proposal, two client calls, gym, meal prep — into a time-blocked day with realistic durations and buffers."

### 🤝 Schedule meetings and appointments

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me write a clear message to schedule [meeting type] with [person], offering a few time options.
- I have these meetings to fit in this week: [list]. Suggest a schedule that protects my focus time.
- Suggest a policy for how I accept, batch, or decline meeting requests as a [role].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I schedule meetings without fragmenting my day?"
- "What's the best way to propose meeting times politely?"
- "How can I keep meetings short and effective?"
- "How do I reduce the number of meetings I attend?"
- "How should I batch meetings to protect deep work?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Help me write a clear message to schedule a project kickoff with a new client, offering a few time options."

## 📚 Education

### 📘 Recommend learning strategies

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- I'm trying to learn [subject/skill] and retain it long-term. Recommend evidence-based learning strategies for me.
- Based on the fact that I have [time available] and learn best by [doing/reading/listening], suggest a study approach for [topic].
- Help me build a learning plan for [subject] that uses active recall and spaced repetition.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the most effective, research-backed ways to learn?"
- "How do active recall and spaced repetition work?"
- "How do I retain what I learn instead of forgetting it?"
- "How do I learn faster without sacrificing depth?"
- "What's the best way to learn a practical skill versus a theoretical one?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "I'm trying to learn Spanish and retain it long-term. Recommend evidence-based learning strategies for me."

---

### 🚀 Provide educational feedback

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Here's my work on [subject]: [paste]. Give me detailed feedback and explain my mistakes so I understand them.
- Act as a tutor for [subject]. Quiz me on [topic], then give feedback on my answers.
- Review my understanding of [concept] by checking this explanation I wrote: [paste].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How can I get useful feedback on my learning when studying alone?"
- "What's the best way to learn from my mistakes?"
- "How do I know if I've truly understood a concept?"
- "How can I test myself effectively?"
- "How do I close gaps in my knowledge efficiently?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Act as a tutor for statistics. Quiz me on hypothesis testing, then give feedback on my answers."

<!-- ==================== NEXT GUIDE / PART ==================== -->

# 🎯 The Coach's Prompts for Claude

> **How to use this guide:** Copy any prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders with your details, and paste it into Claude (free or paid).
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** produce structured, ready-to-use output.
> - **Question-based prompts** help you explore and go deeper.

---

## 📘 Facebook Organic

### 💫 Generating Ideas for Facebook Posts

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Generate [number] Facebook post ideas for my [niche] coaching business that will engage [target audience].
- I help [audience] achieve [result]. Suggest [number] post ideas that mix value, story, and promotion.
- Give me a week of Facebook post ideas around the theme of [topic], with a hook for each.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What types of Facebook posts get the most engagement for coaches?"
- "How do I balance value, personal stories, and promotion in my posts?"
- "What makes a Facebook post stop the scroll?"
- "How often should I post on Facebook to grow organically?"
- "How do I turn a single idea into multiple posts?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Generate 10 Facebook post ideas for my fitness coaching business that will engage busy parents."

---

### 🎮 Facebook Content Strategy

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Build a 30-day Facebook content strategy for my [niche] coaching business with the goal of [goal].
- Help me define content pillars for my Facebook page targeting [audience].
- Create a weekly posting plan mixing content types (value, story, engagement, promo) for [niche].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What does an effective Facebook content strategy look like for a coach?"
- "How many content pillars should I have and what should they be?"
- "How do I plan content that builds toward selling my offer?"
- "How do I measure whether my Facebook strategy is working?"
- "How do I stay consistent without burning out on content?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Build a 30-day Facebook content strategy for my career-coaching business with the goal of booking discovery calls."

---

### 📄 Creating Descriptions for Pages and Groups

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Write a compelling Facebook Page description for my [niche] coaching business that conveys [value/promise].
- Write a Facebook Group description that attracts [target members] and sets clear expectations.
- Create an "About" section for my page that builds trust and includes a call to action to [action].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What should a great Facebook Page or Group description include?"
- "How do I make my group description attract the right members?"
- "How do I communicate my value clearly in a short description?"
- "What call to action works best in a page description?"
- "How do I use keywords so my page/group gets found?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Write a Facebook Group description that attracts new entrepreneurs and sets clear expectations for a supportive, no-spam community."

---

### 👥 Engaging in Facebook Groups

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

### 💼 Writing Job Descriptions

  6. A Call-To-Action (CTA) inviting candidates to apply.
  We are looking for a person who [describe the ideal candidate].
- Present top ways to write a job description that is optimized for search engines to attract more candidates for the [job role] in the [industry] industry.
- My [industry] business is looking for someone who [responsibilities/qualities]. We need someone who has [time of experience] in the field. We offer: [benefit 1], [benefit 2], and [benefit 3]. This is a [Full-Time/Part-Time] [Remote/On-Site] position.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "Can you help me write an effective job description that will attract qualified candidates?"
- "What are some best practices for writing a job description that accurately reflects the responsibilities and requirements of the position?"
- "How can I ensure that my job description is clear and concise while also being detailed enough to give candidates a good understanding of the role?"
- "What are some common mistakes to avoid when writing a job description?"
- "Can you provide guidance on how to write a job description that is inclusive and avoids bias?"
- "How can I ensure that my job description complies with relevant labor laws and regulations?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Write me a job description for a part-time community manager for my online coaching membership, including intro, responsibilities, qualifications, experience, compensation, and a CTA."

---

- Create behavioral interview questions for [role].

<!-- ==================== NEXT GUIDE / PART ==================== -->

# 📣 The Marketer's Prompts for Claude

> **How to use this guide:** Copy any prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders with your details, and paste it into Claude (free or paid).
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** produce structured, ready-to-use output.
> - **Question-based prompts** help you explore and go deeper.

---

## 🧰 General Business Toolkit

### 💥 Researching Your Competitors

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me analyze my competitors in the [industry] space. My main competitors are [list]. Compare their positioning, offers, and messaging.
- Create a competitor analysis framework for [niche], covering strengths, weaknesses, and gaps I could exploit.
- Based on this competitor's website/offer — [paste/describe] — identify what they do well and where I could differentiate.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What's the best way to research competitors in my industry?"
- "What should I look for when analyzing a competitor's marketing?"
- "How do I find gaps in the market my competitors miss?"
- "How do I differentiate without just copying competitors?"
- "How often should I review the competitive landscape?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Help me analyze my competitors in the online fitness coaching space. My main competitors are [list]. Compare their positioning, offers, and messaging."

---

### 🏦 Creating a Business Plan

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me draft a business plan for my [business type] targeting [audience], covering offer, market, marketing, and revenue.
- Create a one-page business plan for [business idea].
- Outline the key sections of a business plan and help me fill them in for [business].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What are the essential components of a business plan?"
- "How detailed should a business plan be for a small business?"
- "How do I define my target market in a business plan?"
- "How do I create realistic financial projections?"
- "How do I keep a business plan flexible as things change?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Create a one-page business plan for a subscription box for eco-friendly products."

# 🚀 The Ultimate Prompts for Claude

> **How to use this guide:** Copy any prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders with your details, and paste it into Claude (free or paid).
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** produce structured, ready-to-use output.
> - **Question-based prompts** help you explore and go deeper.
>
> Browse the 19 categories below — marketing, writing, social media, operations, and more.

---

## 1. 📣 Content Marketing

- Develop a content strategy for my [business] targeting [audience], with goals, pillars, formats, and channels.
- Create a [time frame] content plan to grow [metric] for [niche].
- Define [number] content pillars and example topics for [brand].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What makes a content strategy effective?"
- "How do I define content pillars?"
- "How do I align content with business goals?"
- "How do I measure content performance?"
- "How do I stay consistent with content?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Develop a content strategy for my SaaS targeting marketing managers, with goals, pillars, formats, and channels."

- Suggest which processes in my [business] should be standardized first.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "Why standardize processes and when?"
- "How do I write a clear SOP?"
- "Which processes should I document first?"
- "How do I keep SOPs up to date?"
- "How does standardization help me scale?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Document this process into clear, repeatable steps: how I publish a blog post."

<!-- ==================== NEXT GUIDE / PART ==================== -->

# 💼 The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude — Part 1: Core Business

> **How to use this guide:** Copy any prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders with your details, and paste it into Claude (free or paid).
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** produce structured, ready-to-use output.
> - **Question-based prompts** help you explore and go deeper.
>
> *This is Part 1 of the Business Owner's guide (Core Business). Further parts cover Customer Service & Sales, Real Estate & Property Management, Lead Generation & Nurturing, HR, and Support.*

---

## 📈 Growth Strategy & General Business

### 📈 Setting up Metrics for Your Business

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me identify the key metrics to track for my [business type] at the [stage] stage.
- Suggest a simple dashboard of metrics to measure growth and health for [business].
- Based on my goal of [goal], which 3-5 metrics should I focus on and why?

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "What metrics matter most for a business like mine?"
- "How do I choose between vanity metrics and real KPIs?"
- "How often should I review my business metrics?"
- "How do I set targets for each metric?"
- "How do I turn metrics into decisions?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Help me identify the key metrics to track for my e-commerce store at the early-growth stage."

---

### 👀 Researching Competitors

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me analyze my competitors in [industry]. My main competitors are [list]. Compare positioning, offers, and pricing.
- Create a competitor analysis framework for [niche] and identify gaps I could exploit.
- Based on this competitor — [describe] — what do they do well and where could I differentiate?

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I research competitors effectively?"
- "What should I analyze about a competitor?"
- "How do I find gaps competitors are missing?"
- "How do I differentiate without copying?"
- "How often should I review the competition?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Create a competitor analysis framework for the meal-delivery niche and identify gaps I could exploit."

---

### 🎯 Launching a Product

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Create a product launch plan for [product] targeting [audience], covering pre-launch, launch, and post-launch.
- Suggest a launch strategy to maximize sales of [product].

### 🏷 Preparing for Taxes

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me create a checklist to prepare for taxes for my [business type].
- Suggest records and documents I should organize before tax season.
- Help me understand common deductions for a [business type] (general guidance).

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I prepare my business for tax season?"
- "What records should I keep for taxes?"
- "What deductions might apply to my business?"
- "How do I stay organized year-round for taxes?"
- "When should I work with an accountant?"

- *Filled-in example:* "Suggest records and documents I should organize before tax season for a freelance business."

*Note: For your specific tax situation, consult a qualified accountant or tax professional.*

# 💼 The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude — Part 2: Customer Service, Sales, Networking & Team

> **How to use this guide:** Copy a prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders, and paste into Claude.

>
> *Part 2 of the Business Owner's guide.*

# 💼 The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude — Part 9: Human Resources (A) — Recruiting, Onboarding, Performance & Development

> **How to use this guide:** Copy a prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders, and paste into Claude.
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** give structured output. **Question-based prompts** help you explore.
>

> *Note: HR documents and policies have legal implications that vary by jurisdiction — have qualified HR/legal professionals review anything binding.*

---

- *Filled-in example:* "Suggest where to find qualified software engineers and what they expect."

### 📶 Creating Social Media Recruiting Campaigns

- Create a social media recruiting campaign to attract [role] candidates.

- "Which platforms work best for recruiting?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Write posts promoting a marketing manager opening that showcase our culture."

# 💼 The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude — Part 10: Human Resources (B) — Workforce, HR Tech, Data & Compliance

> **How to use this guide:** Copy a prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders, and paste into Claude.
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** give structured output. **Question-based prompts** help you explore.
>
> *Part 10 of the Business Owner's guide.*
> *Note: HR policies and compliance vary by jurisdiction — have qualified HR/legal professionals review anything binding.*

---

## 📆 Workforce Planning

### 📆 Creating Workforce Plans & Headcount Planning

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Map which roles to hire and when to reach [objective].

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I plan my workforce for growth?"
- "How do I decide what roles to hire and when?"
- "How do I align headcount with budget?"
- "How do I avoid over- or under-hiring?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Suggest a headcount plan for the next 12 months to scale from 15 to 30 employees."

# 💼 The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude — Part 11: Customer Support (Phone, Chat, Email, Chatbots)

> **How to use this guide:** Copy a prompt, replace the `[bracketed]` placeholders, and paste into Claude.
> - **Fill-in-the-blank prompts** give structured output. **Question-based prompts** help you explore.
>
> *Part 11 (final) of the Business Owner's guide. The source's Support I–V sections repeat the same skills across phone, chat, and email — this consolidates them into channel-agnostic groups. Where a prompt is channel-specific, just swap in "[phone/chat/email]".*

---

## 🎧 Core Support Skills

### 🪄 Resolving Customer Issues Efficiently

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Suggest a step-by-step approach to solve [common issue] for customers.
- Draft a [phone/chat/email] response that resolves [issue] and reassures the customer.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I resolve customer issues quickly without cutting corners?"
- "How do I balance speed and quality in support?"
- "How do I handle issues I can't immediately solve?"
- "How do I leave customers satisfied after a problem?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Draft a chat response that resolves a 'my order hasn't arrived' issue and reassures the customer."

- *Filled-in example:* "Identify recurring issues and root causes from this data: most tickets are about login problems and slow shipping."

### 🎸 Monitoring Brand Mentions & Using User-Generated Content

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Suggest how to monitor and respond to brand mentions across channels.
- Help me create a process for engaging with user-generated content.
- Draft responses to positive and negative public mentions.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I monitor brand mentions?"
- "How do I respond to public mentions well?"
- "How do I leverage user-generated content?"
- "How do I turn mentions into engagement?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Draft responses to positive and negative public mentions of my brand."

---

### 🔐 Offering Online Security & Account Guidance

**FILL-IN-THE-BLANK PROMPTS:**

- Help me write guidance for customers on keeping their accounts secure.
- Draft a response for a customer worried about [security concern].
- Create security best-practice tips to share with customers.

**QUESTIONS-BASED PROMPTS:**

- "How do I help customers stay secure?"
- "How do I respond to security concerns?"
- "How do I guide customers on account safety?"
- "How do I handle suspected fraud reports?"

**EXAMPLES:**

- *Filled-in example:* "Draft a response for a customer worried their account was accessed without permission."

*End of Part 11 — and the end of **The Business Owner's Prompts for Claude**.*
